- 3556 repository URLs were included in the corpus being tested
- 1005 repository URLs in the corpus were skipped because they were duplicated

- 0.08% of repository URLs contain one or more Error level issue
- 0.00% of repository URLs contain one or more Warning level issue
- 0.00% of repository URLs contain one or more Notice level issue
- 117ms average time it took to download each certificate
